class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><font size="3"><strong><span>Model 930 Jerry Miculek JM Pro Series 12 Gauge 3 Inch Chamber 22 Inch Vent Rib Barrel Black Synthetic Stock 8 Round</span></strong></font><p></p> <p><font size="3"><strong><span><span>Competition level engineering. Features a beveled loading gate and shortened forend for ease of loading and an added barrel clamp for extended mag tube stability. Dual gas system for recoil reduction. Accu-set choke tubes includes Full, Modified and Improved Cylinder. Engraved receiver. Knurled charging handle for retracting the bolt. Quick-empy magazine button for unloading. Matte blue vent-rib barrel. Black synthetic stock and forend with checkering. Fiber optic front sight. Three inch chamber. Gun lock included.</span><br></span></strong></font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="2"><em>Jerry Miculek is a world renowned competitive and speed shooter having won</em></font><br><font size="2"><em>dozens of National and World shooting titles. The JM Pro Series 930</em></font><br><font size="2"><em>features a beveled loading gate, shorter forend, and barrel clamp for</em></font><br><font size="2"><em>maximum stabilization and the quickest loading times. This Miculek model</em></font><br><font size="2"><em>also features a 22" barrel and 9 shot capacity and receiver engraving.</em></font></p> <p><font size="2">In the world of competitive shooting, the name Jerry Miculek is synonymous with record breaking success. A highly-accomplished shooter and five-time USPSA 3-Gun National Championship winner, Miculek depends on his equipment to reliably-deliver when fractions of seconds count. Now you can shoot the&nbsp;same shotgun that this legendary champion uses as Mossberg proudly announces the JM Pro Series 930&nbsp;Tactical Class of signature shotguns. </font></p> <p><font size="2">Initial offerings in this series of competition-oriented autoloaders include 10-shot and 9-shot versions with many performance-enhancing features. Further distinguishing this signature&nbsp;series is the JM Pro Series Tactical Class logo laser-engraved on the receiver. The versatile 930 platform features a dual gas-vent operating system which aids in recoil reduction and&nbsp;reduces stress and wear on operating parts. &nbsp;This 12 gauge semi-auto reliably handles 2 and 3-inch from&nbsp;low-brass target loads to hard-hitting magnum rounds. </font></p> <p><font size="2">Standard features include Uni-Linestock and receiver&nbsp;design for instinctive eye/rib alignment; stock drop spacer system for customizing fit; &nbsp;drilled and tapped&nbsp;receiver; interchangeable ACCU-CHOKEsystem; durable black synthetic stock and forend; and matte blue&nbsp;metal finishes.</font></p> <p><font size="2">Performance-enhancing features on the JM Pro Series include Mossbergs extended tactical bolt handle;&nbsp;forend cut to facilitate faster reloads; oversized safety button; orange magazine follower; and protective barrel&nbsp;clamp for the extended mag tube. The 10-Shot Tactical Class has a 24-inch, non-ported, vent rib barrel with&nbsp;standard ACCU-CHOKE Modified tube; red fiber optic front bead sight; extended 9-shot magazine tube;adjustable trigger stop; &nbsp;and &nbsp;anodized receiver with chamfered loading port opening. &nbsp; </font></p> <p><font size="2">Winning a national championship or setting a world record may not be in the cards for you. Looking like a&nbsp;champion and shooting the same gun that world-renown shooter, Jerry Miculek does is possible with the new&nbsp;Mossberg JM Pro Series 930 Signature Shotguns.</font></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Shotguns</li><li>Action : Semi-Automatic</li><li>Gauge : 12 Gauge</li><li>Barrel Length : 22.0"</li><li>Capacity : 8+1</li><li>Chamber : 3"</li><li>OAL : 42.5"</li><li>Weight : 7.75 lbs</li><li>Choke Configuration : Accu-Choke</li><li>Receiver Description : Black</li><li>Stock Description : Black Synthetic</li></ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">1</span> customer </span>&nbsp;
